## Diagram 3

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Build
    Build --> dev1: on_success
    Build --> dev2: on_success
    Build --> qa1: manual/RELEASE
    Build --> qa2: manual/RELEASE
    Build --> staging1: manual/RELEASE
    Build --> test: manual/RELEASE
    Build --> prod_b: manual/RELEASE
    
    dev1 --> Release
    dev2 --> Release
    qa1 --> Release
    qa2 --> Release
    staging1 --> Release
    test --> Release
    prod_b --> Release
    
    Release --> tag: RELEASE=true
    tag --> [*]
```
